| Feature                                           | Epic                                                                                                   | Description                                                                                                                                              | Result                                                                                                                                                    |
| ------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Detail proposal pada unit pengelola               | informasi proposal                                                                                     | admin dapat melihat id proposal                                                                                                                          | Berhasil Menampilkan id proposal                                                                                                                          |
|                                                   |                                                                                                        | admin dapat melihat judul proposal                                                                                                                       | Berhasil Menampilkan judul proposal                                                                                                                       |
